再找 $S_{k}(R)$ 与 $S_{k - 1}(R)$ 间，及 $V_{k}(R)$ 与 $V_{k - 1}(R)$ 间的递归关系.

先取 $k = 3$ 作具体分析.3维球如图附-14所示，将它分解成一系列厚为 $\left|\mathrm{dz}\right|$ ，圆半径记为 $r = R\sin \phi$ 的薄圆板.因 $z = R\cos \phi$ ，即有

$$
| \mathrm{d} z | = R \sin \phi \mathrm{d} \phi ,
$$

薄圆板的圆周长和圆面积是半径 r 的 2 维球的面积 $S_{2}(r)$ 和体积 $V_{2}(r)$ ，薄圆板侧面积 $dS_{板}$ 和体积 $dV_{板}$ 各为

![image](https://cdn-mineru.openxlab.org.cn/result/2026-06-09/a529e936-5eb4-455b-aa5f-b3d8bce6c05a/779bf01d3041be4d508054f2dfd76c4c0cf7e5eda5064de7ace4016a8ccee0e6.jpg)



图 附-14


$$
\mathrm{d} S _ {\text {板}} = S _ {2} (r) R \mathrm{d} \phi = S _ {2} (R \sin \phi) R \mathrm{d} \phi ,
$$

$$
\mathrm{d} V _ {\text {板}} = V _ {2} (r) \left| \mathrm{d} z \right| = V _ {2} (R \sin \phi) R \sin \phi \mathrm{d} \phi .
$$

积分得 3 维球面积和体积：

$$
S _ {3} (R) = \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \mathrm{d} S _ {\text {板}} = \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} S _ {2} (R \sin \phi) R \mathrm{d} \phi ,
$$

$$
V _ {3} (R) = \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \mathrm{d} V _ {\text {板}} = \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} V _ {2} (R \sin \phi) R \sin \phi \mathrm{d} \phi .
$$

k 维空间球仍可用图附-14 中的圆代表, 同样将它分解为一系列厚为 $\left|dz\right|$ 的 k 维薄“板”, 图中用两条平行直线间的区域表示. 每一直线段对应半径 $r = R \sin \phi$ 的 k - 1 维球体, 它的面积和体积分别是 $S_{k-1}(r)$ 和 $V_{k-1}(r)$ . 薄“板”侧面积和体积分别为

$$
\mathrm{d} S _ {\text {板}} = S _ {k - 1} (r) R \mathrm{d} \phi = S _ {k - 1} (R \sin \phi) R \mathrm{d} \phi ,
$$

$$
\mathrm{d} V _ {\text {板}} = V _ {k - 1} (r) \left| \mathrm{d} z \right| = V _ {k - 1} (R \sin \phi) R \sin \phi \mathrm{d} \phi .
$$

积分得 $k$ 维球面积和体积：

$$
S _ {k} (R) = \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \mathrm{d} S _ {\text {板}} = \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} S _ {k - 1} (R \sin \phi) R \mathrm{d} \phi ,
$$

$$
V _ {k} (R) = \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \mathrm{d} V _ {\text {板}} = \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} V _ {k - 1} (R \sin \phi) R \sin \phi \mathrm{d} \phi .
$$

k 维球面积和体积必定分别与 $R^{k-1}$ 和 $R^{k}$ 成正比, 可表达成

$$
S _ {k} (R) = A _ {k} R ^ {k - 1}, \quad V _ {k} (R) = B _ {k} R ^ {k},
$$

得

$$
S _ {k} (R \sin \phi) = A _ {k} R ^ {k - 1} \sin^ {k - 1} \phi = S _ {k} (R) \sin^ {k - 1} \phi ,
$$

$$
V _ {k} (R \sin \phi) = B _ {k} R ^ {k} \sin^ {k} \phi = V _ {k} (R) \sin^ {k} \phi .
$$

结合前述公式,便有

$$
S _ {k} (R) = S _ {k - 1} (R) R \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \sin^ {k - 2} \phi d \phi , \tag {②}
$$

$$
V _ {k} (R) = V _ {k - 1} (R) R \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \sin^ {k} \phi \mathrm{d} \phi , \tag {③}
$$

这就是 k 维球与 k-1 维球之间的递归关系.

关于 $S_{k}(R)$ 和 $V_{k}(R)$ 表达式：

由③式可得

$$
V _ {k - 2} (R) = V _ {k - 3} (R) R \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \sin^ {k - 2} \phi d \phi ,
$$

与②式联立，便有

$$
S _ {k} (R) = S _ {k - 1} (R) \frac {V _ {k - 2} (R)}{V _ {k - 3} (R)},
$$

结合①式,得

$$
S _ {k} (R) = \frac {S _ {k - 1} (R) S _ {k - 2} (R) (k - 3)}{S _ {k - 3} (R) (k - 2)}. \tag {4}
$$

取 $k = 2N + 1$ ，由④式得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \frac {S _ {2 N + 1} (R)}{S _ {2 N - 1} (R)} = \frac {2 N - 2}{2 N - 1} \cdot \frac {S _ {2 N} (R)}{S _ {2 N - 2} (R)} \\ = \frac {2 N - 2}{2 N - 1} \cdot \frac {2 N - 3}{2 N - 2} \cdot \dots \cdot \frac {1}{2} \cdot \frac {S _ {3} (R)}{S _ {1} (R)}, \\ \end{array}
$$

即

$$
S _ {2 N + 1} (R) = \frac {1}{2 N - 1} \cdot \frac {S _ {3} (R)}{S _ {1} (R)} S _ {2 N - 1} (R),
$$

当 $N = 1$ ， $S_{3}(R) = \frac{1}{1}\cdot \frac{S_{3}(R)}{S_{1}(R)}\cdot S_{1}(R),$ 

可得

$$
S _ {2 N + 1} (R) = \frac {1}{(2 N - 1) (2 N - 3) \cdot \cdots \cdot 1} \left[ \frac {S _ {3} (R)}{S _ {1} (R)} \right] ^ {N} S _ {1} (R),
$$

即为 $S_{2N + 1}(R) = \frac{2^N(N!)}{(2N)!}\Big[\frac{S_3(R)}{S_1(R)}\Big]^N S_1(R).$ ⑤

再将④式中 k 取为 $2N+2$ ，写出

$$
\frac {S _ {2 N + 2} (R)}{S _ {2 N} (R)} = \frac {2 N - 1}{2 N} \cdot \frac {S _ {2 N + 1} (R)}{S _ {2 N - 1} (R)}
$$

后，可推得

$$
S _ {2 N + 2} (R) = \frac {1}{2 ^ {N} \cdot (N !)} \cdot \left[ \frac {S _ {3} (R)}{S _ {1} (R)} \right] ^ {N} S _ {2} (R), \tag {6}
$$

将⑤⑥①结合,可得

$$
V _ {2 N + 1} (R) = \frac {2 ^ {N} (N !)}{(2 N + 1) !} R \Big [ \frac {S _ {3} (R)}{S _ {1} (R)} \Big ] ^ {N} S _ {1} (R), \tag {7}
$$

$$
V _ {2 N + 2} (R) = \frac {1}{2 ^ {N + 1} [ (N + 1) ! ]} R \left[ \frac {S _ {3} (R)}{S _ {1} (R)} \right] ^ {N} S _ {2} (R). \tag {8}
$$

最后，将

$$
S _ {1} (R) = 2, \quad S _ {2} (R) = 2 \pi R, \quad S _ {3} (R) = 4 \pi R ^ {2}
$$

代入⑤⑥⑦⑧式,即得

$$
S _ {2 N + 2} (R) = \frac {2}{N !} \pi^ {N + 1} R ^ {2 N + 1}, \quad N = 0, 1, 2, \dots ,
$$

$$
V _ {2 N + 2} (R) = \frac {1}{(N + 1) !} \pi^ {N + 1} R ^ {2 N + 2}, \quad N = 0, 1, 2, \dots ,
$$

$$
S _ {2 N + 1} (R) = \frac {2 ^ {2 N + 1} (N !)}{(2 N) !} \pi^ {N} R ^ {2 N}, \qquad \qquad N = 0, 1, 2, \dots ,
$$

$$
V _ {2 N + 1} (R) = \frac {2 ^ {2 N + 1} (N !)}{(2 N + 1) !} \pi^ {N} R ^ {2 N + 1}, \qquad N = 0, 1, 2, \dots .
$$

顺便一提，由导得的 $S_{k}(R)$ 和 $V_{k}(R)$ 表达式，也可获得定积分

$$
\int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \sin^ {k} \phi \mathrm{d} \phi , \quad k = 1, 2, \dots
$$

表达式, 对 k=2,3,4, 可借用附-14 解答进行验证, 此处从略.
